Current Affairs Commentary

The World's Raw Material Distribution Problem 43

— Dao

In recent days, many British and American politicians have raised the issue of raw material distribution. In the United States, Secretary of State Hull advocated opening up the world's raw materials so that countries lacking raw materials can obtain them peacefully without resorting to military force. In the United Kingdom, former Labour Party leader Lansbury expressed the view that the only way to eliminate today's world crisis is to redistribute the world's raw materials, and the method is to redistribute the world's colonies. Former Prime Minister Lloyd George even supported Lansbury's proposal to reconsider the League of Nations mandate territories. These politicians have recognized the struggle for raw materials as an important factor in war and are seeking ways to resolve it.

Although both Hull and Lansbury's arguments focus on the distribution of raw materials, their methods are very different. Hull advocates the free flow of world raw materials through international agreements, while Lansbury focuses on the redistribution of colonies. We have not yet seen the details of these two proposals, and the proponents may not even have concrete solutions. However, the advantages and disadvantages are already obvious. Hull's proposal is relatively fair, while Lansbury's proposal is tantamount to military plunder. Why is it that international figures today oppose aggressive countries because they oppose their treatment of people in colonies? Although the proposal to redistribute colonies does not openly encourage military aggression, it tacitly acknowledges the legitimacy of their actions. This is one reason. Secondly, the so-called redistribution of colonies means that countries with too many colonies should divide some of them to countries lacking colonies to show balance. This may be a generous and elegant action when strong countries transfer territories to each other, but it greatly disregards the personality of the colonial people. This is the second reason. Thirdly, a truly just international proposal should abolish colonies altogether and seek to communicate raw materials through purely trade methods. We do not yet know whether the contradictions and conflicts between the great powers can be eliminated, and the identity of colonies will never be resolved. This is the third reason.

However, the actual value of these two proposals is questionable. The reason why ambitious countries today do not hesitate to invade other countries by force is that on the one hand, they are competing for raw materials, and on the other hand, they are competing for markets. Therefore, colonies are not only a source of raw materials for imperialists but also a market for imperialists to sell goods. The reason why raw materials are in great demand is nothing more than to maintain or expand their domestic industry. If imperialists abandon part of their inherent colonies, the maintenance and expansion of their domestic industry will become a problem due to the loss of part of the market. Moreover, as current facts show, countries are trying to block markets within their sphere of influence and are trying their best to compete for markets beyond their reach. The former uses the method of building high tariff barriers in their own country to make it difficult for goods from other countries to enter, while the latter uses the method of currency devaluation and exchange dumping. Today's great powers are intent on using these two weapons and will never look back. To say that they can discuss the redistribution of colonies is to be ignorant of the truth of the matter. As for Hull's proposal, it is considered too lofty and difficult to achieve results. It includes not only the distribution of raw materials but also the distribution of markets. How the market will be distributed in what proportion is a major problem.

In short, Lansbury's method is a method of replacing violence with violence. This kind of method may be generous between strong countries, but it only shows its unkindness to weak and helpless nations. As for Hull's method, considering the setbacks of the 1933 World Economic Conference and the current naval conference, it is feared that there will be no good results.

Soviet Russian Military Deployment in the Far East 44

Cooperating with Outer Mongolia for Defense

Harbin. Since the intensification of the disputes between Japan, the puppet state, Soviet Russia, and Mongolia, the Soviet Union, fearing that Japanese and puppet troops would pressure Outer Mongolia from Inner Mongolia and attack the Soviet Union, has stationed troops on the border between Inner and Outer Mongolia to cooperate with the Mongolian army for defense. Currently, the military preparations between Kulun and Ude are the responsibility of the Second Battalion of the 48th Regiment of the 25th Brigade of the 14th Division of the Far Eastern Red Army. The battalion headquarters is located in Ude, including Motezhen (one company), Kololo San (forty people), Okomoer (two companies), Bisierge (thirty people), Bielgete (twenty people), Xiong Youluomo Osk (two companies), Uyula (thirty people), Senzhi (twenty people), and Ude (battalion headquarters). The battalion has two reconnaissance planes, ten fighter planes, one light bomber, and one heavy bomber. The standing air force is also equipped with dozens of machine guns and field guns, and five forts have been built. More than thirty large trucks regularly travel between Kulun and Ude, exclusively for military use. There is also regular air service between Kulun and Ude, with a flight time of only two to three hours. The military equipment of the Kulun Army includes the headquarters of the 14th Division of the Red Army and the headquarters of the 48th Regiment, with a force of three to four thousand. The air force has thirty-two heavy bombers, twenty-four light bombers, fifty-one fighter planes, and thirteen reconnaissance planes, totaling two hundred. In terms of artillery, there are fifteen howitzers and forty field guns, as well as a number of mortars and armored vehicles. The recently increased Red Army and sophisticated weapons stationed there are not included. (8th China United Press Telegram)

Harbin. People in Harbin are greatly disturbed by the news of Soviet Russian military preparations in Siberia. According to the Daily News, the Soviet Russian Minister of Communications has issued an instruction that all personnel employed by the Siberian Railway, except for communists and communist youth league members, should be withdrawn to the Russian territory in Asia. It is reported that the Soviet Russian military authorities are now taking over all railways in Siberia and have taken over the full management of the Outer Baikal line. It is also reported that the Soviet Russian authorities are setting up a railway and military office in Chita. The Harbin Defense Association, in order to protect Harbin from air raids, has organized eleven militia teams, totaling three thousand people, to train and use anti-poisoning equipment and anti-aircraft artillery. (8th Reuters Telegram)

Moscow. Due to the prevalence of epidemics in Manchuria, the border between the Soviet Union and "Manchukuo" along the Heilongjiang River from Gumar to Bashkovo had been closed to traffic. The Soviet government has now decided to resume traffic there because the epidemics have disappeared. (8th TASS Telegram)

Moscow. The Russian newspaper Pravda, in today's editorial, said regarding the recent border conflicts, "We must station an entire army group on the 'Manchukuo' border to prevent the Japanese from carrying machine guns into Russian territory. The Soviet Russian side is currently not organizing an expedition to Manchuria." The newspaper warned against those who disrupt peace in the Far East. (8th Reuters Telegram)

US New Agricultural Law Committee Passes Report 45

Washington. The House Agriculture Committee today presented a report in favor of the government's agricultural bill. The committee chairman Jones and a majority of members recommended passing the bill and stated that the bill could legally resolve the agricultural problems arising from the failure of the Agricultural Adjustment Act. However, a minority of members of the committee dissented, saying that the Secretary of Agriculture Wallace would gain great power because of the bill. Congressman Pooley also presented a report saying that the bill would harm milk merchants in the Midwest and East. (7th National News Agency Telegram)

Washington. Although many Democratic and Republican congressmen doubt that the Agricultural Adjustment Act replacement bill is constitutional, Senate Majority Leader Robinson today predicted that the bill could be passed in the Senate early next week. (7th Reuters Telegram)

New York. Davis' assistant, Burt, the Agricultural Adjustment Commissioner, said today that the US government would not dump cotton obtained from the implementation of agricultural controls. If Congress passes the government's new agricultural bill, cotton production will still be controlled from 1936 onwards. Government officials only want to sell a sufficient amount of cotton to meet commercial needs. (7th National News Agency Telegram)

Washington. Jones, the president of the Financial Reconstruction Corporation, told reporters today that loaned cotton would not be sold on the market until the new rural program was fully formulated and the future path was clearly defined. (7th Reuters Telegram)

Washington. President Roosevelt said today that the question of how to raise funds to pay for veterans' benefits has not yet been resolved, which requires 500 million yuan in tax revenue. As for how much relief funds are needed, it is currently difficult to determine. However, the government is currently studying whether it can use current funds for relief or use funds from other departments. In the future, it may be possible to use funds from the Army, Navy, Labor Department, and Commerce Department. (7th National News Agency Telegram)

Washington. The Federal Reserve Board announced today that the gold reserves of the Federal Reserve Banks decreased by $11,000,000 in the week before February 5, and the current reserves are $10,168,000,000. This decrease was due to the outflow of gold reserves due to the devaluation of the US dollar, but the preparation of gold bonds increased by $20,000,000. The deposits of foreign banks in New York member banks decreased by $21,000,000, and currently total $379,000,000. The deposits of foreign central banks totaled $66,000,000 on February 5. The reserves of member banks exceeded the legal requirements by $3,090,000,000, which is the same as last week. (7th National News Agency Telegram)

Washington DC Snowfall Reaches 15 Inches, Senate Adjourns 46

America, Zhijia Valley. Recently, the central and northern states of the United States have been affected by the northern cold wave, and all highways have been blocked by snow, and traffic has been cut off. Today, a cold wave of minus ten degrees is sweeping in from Canada, and the situation is becoming increasingly serious. The streets of Washington are covered with fifteen inches of snow, and the entire Potomac River is frozen. The Senate also decided to postpone the meeting until Monday next week because the congressmen could not reach the capital. It is reported that the temperature in the coldest place has dropped to 64 degrees below zero. As a result, factories in the central and northern states have stopped work due to lack of coal, and traffic has been completely suspended. (7th National News Agency Telegram)

If the League of Nations Bans Oil, Italy Has Enough for Several Months. Germany Expresses Strict Neutrality 47

Geneva. The Committee of Experts on the League of Nations' Oil Embargo has now reached a conclusion that if the League of Nations implements an oil embargo against Italy, Italy's oil reserves will only be sufficient for several months, at most eight to ten months. The political preparations for the oil embargo will take three to four months to complete. The Committee of Experts' report has not yet been completed. (8th Havas Telegram)

Geneva. The Committee of Experts on the League of Nations' Oil Embargo, believing that Italy might be able to substitute oil with some substitutes once the oil embargo is implemented, appointed a committee to study this issue. After deliberation, the committee has reached a conclusion that Italy, no matter how frugal it is with gasoline, must continue to import a large amount from foreign countries. Even if it is frugal, it will only be about 110,000 tons per year, and it must depend on the following factors: whether Italy can produce the raw materials necessary for refining gasoline within its borders; whether it can import the necessary raw materials from foreign countries; whether Italy can manufacture or import from foreign countries the tools necessary for manufacturing and using liquid fuels to replace heavy oil; and finally, it must depend on Italy's financial situation. (7th Havas Telegram)

Berlin. Political figures believe that if the League of Nations' oil embargo against Italy is implemented, it will not be enough to stop the Italian-Abyssinian War. On the contrary, it may cause Italy to withdraw from the League of Nations, and its relations with the countries that implement sanctions will become increasingly tense. Germany, which has always maintained a neutral attitude towards the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, will continue to strictly maintain neutrality in the future. (8th Havas Telegram)

Geneva. The Committee of Experts on the League of Nations' Oil Embargo previously appointed a committee to study the issue of oil transportation. The report that the committee should submit has been released tonight, and its conclusion is that if the oil embargo against Italy is to be effective, the best way to do so is to prohibit the sale of oil tankers to countries that do not participate in the embargo, so that they cannot help Italy. According to the experts, Italy can only mobilize 82 oil tankers. (7th Havas Telegram)

The Story of Troop Deployment to Defend the Border Passes is Not True

Rome. It is reported that Italy, in order to prove that it has not been detached from European affairs, has redeployed troops to the Brenner Pass area on the Italian-Austrian border. This news has been denied by semi-official sources, who said that if there is to be any organization for Central European issues, it cannot be done without Italy's participation. This has been proven by the recent international talks held in London and Paris. Therefore, there is no need for Italy to redeploy troops to the Brenner Pass. In addition, foreign sources say that at the recent meeting of the Supreme Council of the Fascist Party, some members advocated that Italy's attitude should be more moderate so that the Abyssinian issue can be easily resolved. This news has also been denied by semi-official sources. (7th Havas Telegram)

London. London. Reuters has learned that when French Foreign Minister Flandin recently visited London to attend the funeral of King George, he suggested to British Foreign Secretary Eden that a Mediterranean Pact be concluded. This pact would be like "the Locarno Pact of the Mediterranean." Once established, the additional detachments of the British fleet currently stationed in the Mediterranean could be gradually withdrawn. The proposal was only tentative, but Eden did not agree, saying that Britain could not conclude a non-aggression pact with a country that has clearly become an aggressor, and there is no hope of establishing this pact even after the Abyssinian War ends. It is said that Flandin also explored this proposal with Italy, but Italy also viewed it coldly. Flandin is no longer pursuing other suggestions. (8th Reuters Telegram)

Argument for Redistributing World Resources. British Experts Say It's Difficult to Implement 50

But it has Attracted National Attention in Japan

London. Former Foreign Secretary Sir Samuel Hoare made a speech at the League of Nations General Assembly on September 11 last year, and his conclusion was, "Looking at the current situation, economic issues are more important than political issues. The British government is now prepared to work with all countries to study the method of redistributing world resources and mandate territories." Since the publication of this statement, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has appointed several experts to study the issue of the distribution of world markets and raw materials. According to our reporter, the experts concluded that the main obstacle to this issue lies in the fact that some countries, such as Germany and Italy, are financially exhausted and have no resources to manage even if they obtain colonies. The experts also studied the issue of ceding territory, believing that whether the object of cession is Germany, Italy, other countries without colonies, or countries that have colonies but feel that they are not self-sufficient, the conclusion can be divided into the following two points: Those who make this request are nothing more than politically driven by dictatorship, and their desire for prestige naturally gives rise to a desire for territory. In the current situation, any country can cede colonial territory to other countries, and domestic opposition may not be drastic, to the point of being irreversible. This can be seen in the fact that when Eden, then Minister Without Portfolio and now Foreign Secretary, visited Italy last August, he was willing to cede a strip of British Somaliland along with the port of Zeila to Abyssinia. (7th Havas Telegram)

Tokyo. The British Parliament's debate on the distribution of raw materials and colonies on February 5 has attracted widespread attention in Japan. A spokesman for the Ministry of Foreign Affairs said today in response to questions from foreign journalists that British and other politicians are now paying close attention to the need to redistribute raw materials, colonies, and markets. For the sake of world peace, this is very gratifying. In the past, various international plans have been adopted to maintain peace, such as the balance of power system before the war, the League of Nations Kellogg-Briand Pact after the war, and the non-aggression pact. However, these plans did not pay attention to the real causes of endangering peace. If we want to permanently eliminate the causes of disturbing peace, we must give appropriate consideration to emerging countries. To give an example, there are some countries that are full of vitality but cannot develop in the current international order. It is fair to give these countries the raw materials and markets necessary for their national survival. However, a small number of great powers are now monopolizing vast lands, natural resources, and markets, and adhering to a policy of rejecting others. This situation is not conducive to promoting world peace. (8th Reuters Telegram)

British Economic Envoy Sir Otto Niemeyer Revisits Japan Upon Return 51

Foreign Minister Hirota Welcomes Meeting

Tokyo: Sir Otto Niemeyer, the British government's chief economic advisor, having spent half a year in China and completed his mission, will soon return home. Together with Sir Hughe Knatchbull-Hugessen, the British Ambassador to China, he will submit an on-the-ground report to Prime Minister Stanley Baldwin and Foreign Secretary Anthony Eden, to facilitate a reassessment of Britain's East Asia policy. On his return journey, he will make a stop in Japan, where he is expected to meet with Foreign Minister Hirota and other relevant parties. The Foreign Ministry received informal notification of this plan on the 8th. Last summer, during Niemeyer's transit to China, he visited Japan, stating that he would return after observing China to discuss the adjustment of Sino-British-Japanese relations based on his experience. Considering this pre-arranged plan, the Japanese government has decided to adopt a welcoming attitude. Foreign Minister Hirota intends to use the meeting to thoroughly explain the current state of Sino-Japanese relations, strongly advocate that Sino-Japanese cooperation and amity can genuinely promote world peace, and explain the reasons for this. Furthermore, he will request that the British government have an accurate understanding of East Asian issues. He also intends to frankly seek Niemeyer's opinion on China's currency reform and the Sino-British relationship at that time, and if there is any misunderstanding about British orchestration, he will ask for clarification, to clarify the relationship between China, Britain and Japan. (8th, Domei News Agency)

Over Thirty People Discuss for Eight Hours

Tokuyama: The coal liquefaction industry, a national project, is moving from comprehensive research towards the establishment of a national fuel policy. A fuel conference was held at the Naval Fuel Plant, with the first day of meetings commencing at 9:00 AM on the 7th. Attendees included Director Yamanaka of the Fuel Plant, Director Yamaoka of the Army Maintenance Bureau, representatives from the Army, Navy, Finance Ministry, Ministry of Commerce and Industry, and other relevant ministries, professors from Tokyo University, Kyoto University, Kyushu University, and Osaka University, as well as other authorities, totaling over thirty people. Focusing on the enterprise value of coal liquefaction, they engaged in discussions for eight hours. As a result of careful study, significant progress was made towards a future national fuel policy. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM. After the adjournment, Mr. Sakai, the Fuel Section Chief of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry, stated that specific details could not be disclosed due to military sensitivity. Although the coal liquefaction project is still under research, the meeting achieved substantial results, and the South Manchuria Railway Company will soon undertake this enterprise. London: Sir Eric Phipps, the British Ambassador to Germany, will soon return home to report to the government on Germany's demands for the restoration of colonies and the remilitarization of the Rhineland. According to news from Berlin, the German government has no intention of raising the issue of Rhineland fortification at this time. However, if the French Parliament ratifies the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty (the Chamber of Deputies is scheduled to discuss the treaty on the 11th of this month), Germany will inevitably construct fortifications along the Rhineland as a precautionary measure. Regarding this, it is reported that the British Foreign Office favors establishing a treaty that would restore Germany's full sovereignty over the Rhineland to satisfy its wishes, while reaffirming the obligations stipulated in the Locarno Pact to ensure France's security, thereby resolving the Rhineland issue. Regarding Germany's demand for the restoration of colonies, British public opinion fears that if Germany is entrusted with the administration of certain territories, it may mistreat the indigenous people, thus expressing strong opposition. It is generally believed that the British government, influenced by public opinion, will not consider the colonial issue at present. However, some political figures advocate returning the League of Nations mandated territories to their original countries to establish colonization companies under international management. If this were done, the issue of improving raw material distribution, as demanded by Italy, could be realized. Financial experts, however, believe that participating in such companies would place a heavy financial burden on some countries, such as Italy, and therefore express dissent. (7th, Havas)

He passed through Berlin and held informal talks with German leader Adolf Hitler. According to Berlin news, the topics discussed were Germany's demand for the restoration of colonies and the issue of the remilitarization of the Rhineland. Naval Conference: Discussion on Qualitative Limitations 58

Italian and French Attitudes Remain Firm

London: The expert subcommittee of the General Committee of the Naval Conference met today and adopted the report of the warship definition issue group (content see yesterday's telegram). They then discussed the issue of qualitative limitations. As a result of the meeting, it was generally felt that Italy's attitude on the issue of battleship tonnage was as firm as France's. The US representative was the first to speak today, insisting on the original proposal of 35,000 tons for battleship tonnage, but accepting the British proposal of a 14-inch gun caliber (the US originally proposed 16 inches). Another British proposal was also accepted by the US, namely not building 10,000-ton cruisers for a certain period. However, it was stated that accepting this proposal did not mean that 10,000-ton cruisers would be abolished in the future. The US also expressed support for two proposals, namely classifying Class B cruisers and destroyers as the same type of warship, and limiting submarine tonnage to 2,000 tons (as proposed by the UK). Subsequently, the British representative reiterated the UK's recently stated views, stating that although the UK accepted the figure of 35,000 tons for battleship tonnage, it preferred to reduce it to 25,000 tons, and that 10,000-ton cruisers should be abolished. The French and Italian representatives spoke successively, maintaining their original positions on the battleship tonnage issue (i.e., limiting it to 27,000 tons or 28,000 tons), and supported limiting submarine tonnage to 2,000 tons. The subcommittee is scheduled to continue its meeting on Monday afternoon. (7th, Havas)

London: Delegations participating in the naval conference of the four countries of the United States, Britain, France, and Italy are now engaged in arguing over the form of battleships. At a subcommittee meeting held today, each delegation expressed its views on qualitative limitations. The US delegation requested that battleships be limited to 35,000 tons and equipped with 16-inch caliber guns. However, it stated that the US government was willing to consider setting the gun caliber at 14 inches. The US delegation agreed not to consider 10,000-ton cruisers during the effective period of any treaty and supported the British proposal to limit the maximum tonnage of submarines to 2,000 tons. In short, the four countries participating in the naval conference are almost entirely in agreement on everything except the largest form of battleships. This issue will now be handed over to the chief representatives of the four countries for decision. The UK advocates limiting battleships to 25,000 tons, while France and Italy want to limit them to 27,500 tons. (7th, Reuters)

Order 67

National Government Order on the 8th: The Statute of the 25th Year of the Republic of China Unified Public Debt is hereby formulated and promulgated. This order.

Impressions of the North 68

— Special Correspondent Geng Ya

(10) Tragic Scenes in the Autonomous Vortex

Beiping was the capital of the Liao, Jin, Yuan, Ming, and Qing dynasties. At the beginning of the Republic of China, the central government was still located here. In the sixteenth year of the Republic, the National Government established its capital in Nanjing and renamed Beiping as a city, directly under the Executive Yuan. At the end of last year, the Hebei-Chahar Political Council was established, and Beiping was transferred to its jurisdiction. Its political, cultural, and transportation status in the north has not declined. Unfortunately, it is surrounded by foreign forces, which has become a major problem.

The commercial centers of Beiping are Qianmenwai, Wangfujing Street, and Dong'an Market. The shops outside Qianmen are known for their established brands and long history. The so-called "old residents of Beijing" insist on buying their goods (especially clothing) from there. In recent years, due to changing times, most of these old residents have declined, and commerce outside Qianmen has greatly deteriorated. Wangfujing Street is known for its splendor and grandeur, and its appearance can almost be compared to Nanjing Road in Shanghai. Dong'an Market is known for its delicacy and exquisiteness, with stalls lining the streets and a variety of goods on display, making it even more tempting than Wangfujing. Therefore, general customers, especially modern men and women, prefer to go there. Foreign tourists visiting Beiping also consider a tour of the market a necessary part of their itinerary. The population of Beiping decreased sharply after the capital moved south, but it has been increasing daily since the September 18th Incident. By last year, it had increased to over 1.5645 million people. However, this sharp increase is mostly due to unemployed and impoverished people from the Northeast who have been displaced and moved in, and they have very little purchasing power. At the same time, foreign goods take advantage of Chinese tariffs, lower exchange rates, and are sold cheaply in our markets. Therefore, Dong'an Market is filled with foreign goods, including cosmetics, children's toys, daily household goods, and industrial products. Finding domestic goods is like finding gold in sand. What is shocking is that a young woman in a leather coat wanted to buy domestic goods, and a foreign plainclothes man saw her and dared to slap her in the face in public. Those who wanted to defend her were persuaded to stop. With this situation, the Beiping market will be dominated by foreign goods in the future.

Since last winter, inns and apartments in Beiping have been forcibly rented by foreign ruffians and Koreans for setting up gambling dens and selling drugs. If the landlord inquires, they destroy property and demand compensation. When a gambling den first opened, no one entered, so they came up with the idea of asking the Chamber of Commerce to help maintain it. A prominent merchant could not refuse and invited his friends to gamble, but they all lost tens of thousands of yuan. The drugs they sell are toxins that spread to weaken the country and exterminate the race, and many ignorant compatriots are lured into the fire pit. Officials, probably driven by conscience, obtained the consent of the Japanese police and recently conducted a raid, arresting over 600 opium addicts and gamblers. In the war zone (eastern Hebei), foreign firms are rampant, and drugs are flooding the area. In just two years, 2.8 million people have become addicted to various drugs, with white powder addicts accounting for more than half, totaling 1.5 million people. A certain concession in Tianjin used to be a den of opium, gambling, and drugs. A certain person of importance made a statement upon arrival that he would not investigate opium and gambling. The poison will spread, and it will become the second war zone.

The cost of living in Beiping is the lowest among the six major cities in the country. However, the area has been a political city since ancient times, mainly consuming and producing very little. It is difficult for people to make a living, and there are many poor families. The number of impoverished people eating at congee factories in winter increases greatly every year. After the September 18th Incident, the compatriots who fled from the Northeast to Beiping initially thought that the lost territories would be recovered soon and that they would be able to return home. Unexpectedly, day after day, their hopes turned into dreams. Families below the middle class became increasingly poor, and their lives were as miserable as the bannermen after the Qing Dynasty collapsed. The students from the Northeast were especially brave in the two student movements in Beiping. Later, the students went to various counties to awaken the masses. The wealthier compatriots from the Northeast also took the lead in donating慰勞品. The affection is great, and it is unbearable to describe in detail.

There are over 40,000 rickshaws operating in Beiping, and some are rented out day and night, with two people pulling one rickshaw. But the income is very low. A long pull of more than ten miles usually only earns about ten cents in legal tender. According to a friend from the Northeast, some of the hot-blooded men who had been in the volunteer army, after failing and entering the pass, were forced by life to support themselves by pulling rickshaws. I once heard a rickshaw puller complain that "a foreigner rode in my rickshaw without paying, and when I reported it to the police, I was reprimanded instead." Another rickshaw puller replied loudly, "Who told you to be useless and pull the ______." Is this the hot-blooded man that my friend described?

Liu Xiang: Training County Government Personnel 69

Second Group of Trainees Graduated, Personally Approved by Liu Xiang; Third Group Begins Enrollment

Chengdu News, When the Sichuan Provincial Government was reorganized the year before last, Liu Xiang took charge of provincial administration, making the elimination of excessive taxes and the implementation of a unified tax system the first step in reforming Sichuan's administration. Liu Xiang also recognized that Sichuan had been in turmoil for too long, and that in order to fundamentally reform politics, it was necessary to start with the practical transformation of county government personnel, the so-called "officials who are close to the people." Therefore, last year he established a training institute for county government personnel. When Liu Xiang convened the first group of trainees for instruction, he said, "Throughout history, order and chaos have alternated, and a few individuals have always been the backbone. Because their actions and ideas can win the sympathy and support of the majority, and establish a good model, this becomes the prevailing trend. In the past, during the defense zone system, officials appointed people like bookkeeping, regardless of their talent or lack thereof, and all were appointed. As a result, all kinds of bad things happened, and the superiors had to take responsibility for them. In such cases, the fault lies with the subordinates, but it is not necessarily that the superiors are all good or bad. You should be careful not to disappoint your superiors in your future dealings." He also said, "County government personnel have many things to do, and it is easiest for them to show results. Take the stele of virtuous government as an example; there is not a single county without a stele of virtuous government for the county magistrate, but there are very few people above the county magistrate who are praised by the people. People like Zhuge Wuhou, Luo Wenzhong, and Ding Wencheng are remembered because they made special contributions in Sichuan, so their ancestral temples are still preserved for people to admire. Otherwise, there are not many others. You should administer the people with a public heart, and the local people will never forget you. However, county government personnel are also more miserable than other classes. In counties close to bandit areas, they must assist the army in eliminating the remaining bandits. Local officials have heavy responsibilities, and the local bullies who control local affairs will routinely try to win them over and surround them when a new official arrives. If the county magistrate is confused, he will inevitably be deceived. Once deceived, there will be a day of utter confusion. To sum it up, the combination of theory and practice is essential. The lessons you learn in the institute and the instructions you listen to from your superiors are all theory. After graduation, you will be assigned to positions and seek performance in practice. This is what is called practice. The most important task for Sichuan in the future is to develop the border areas. To do a good job, there is a great shortage of talent. In the future, as long as each of you can take responsibility and be down-to-earth, you can overcome the environment. I hope you will endure hardship and be diligent, not be corrupt, not be slippery, eliminate bad habits, and strive to cultivate virtue and intelligence. Move forward on the broad and bright path, and Sichuan's provincial status and reputation will surely be restored to a great extent." His words were very pertinent, and Liu's deep expectations for county government personnel, the "officials who are close to the people," can also be seen from his speech. The training of these county government personnel, in addition to the first group of personnel being assigned to service after graduation, the second group of personnel has also reached the end of their term and graduated. The list of graduates has been approved by the provincial authorities and posted on the third day of this month. It includes 34 people selected for the county magistrate class, including Zhang Suineng, and 352 people selected for the assistant administrator class, including Zhou Damin (of which Zhou Damin and 13 others had excellent grades, but their qualifications were slightly inferior, so they were temporarily recorded as county magistrates). It is said that the determination of the grades of the graduates was personally made by Liu Xiang as the final approval, and the procedure was extremely careful. According to Deng Mingjie, Secretary-General of the Provincial Government, "At the beginning of his tenure, Chairman Liu was determined to reform the officialdom and believed that governing people was more important than governing laws. Therefore, he first started by breaking the habit of 'appointing people based on personal connections.' He specially requested and was approved by the Military Affairs Commission to establish a civil service qualification review committee, and the entrance examination for the county training institute was also entrusted to it. This time, for the graduation of the second group of students from the county training institute, Liu Xiang took special care. He first ordered the heads of the various departments and the members of the Public Review Committee to conduct oral examinations separately, and secretly draft comments. Finally, Liu Xiang personally conducted oral examinations, referring to the comments of the heads of the various departments and the members of the Public Review Committee to make the final decision. As for the standard of selection, it is purely based on academic qualifications and abilities. Generally speaking, those who are clearly deemed suitable for appointment as county magistrates by the heads of the various departments, the members of the Public Review Committee, and the authorities of the county training institute are included in the county magistrate class. Those whose academic performance and qualifications are only partly acceptable are still included in the assistant administrator class, or those whose academic performance is relatively better are recorded as county magistrates, because their academic qualifications are already excellent, and if they can be further trained, they will achieve even greater achievements in the future. As for those who have more experience as county magistrates, emphasis is placed on their ability to handle affairs, rather than purely on listening and memorizing, which is intended to care for young people on the one hand and value experienced people on the other." In addition, the third group of county training, transferred personnel, on the first day of this month, has already held a written test at the county training institute. More than 200 people came to take the test. On the fifth day of this month, an oral test was held, and on the sixth day, a physical examination was conducted, and then the training was officially started. It is also learned that the written test questions, the first question is to draft a report as a county magistrate of a certain county, listing the long-standing malpractices in the collection of taxes, and proposing methods for rectification, so as to benefit both the national treasury and the people's livelihood; the second question is to draft a proclamation from the provincial government to officials and people throughout the province, advocating propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame, in order to rectify people's hearts and strengthen the foundation of the country.

The Kakuda Incident: Surface Tensions Ease Slightly 70

Our Side Has Raised Questions for Investigation, but Expansion Remains Possible

Shantou Correspondence: Due to the sudden death of Japanese police officer Kakuda in Shantou last month, the situation in Chaoshan suddenly became tense. Although the incident has superficially eased, Lieutenant General Kajikawa stated to others when passing through Shantou on the 29th that this case is of the same nature as the sniping of Japanese sailor Nakayama Hideo in Shanghai. If the feelings between the two sides have not broken down, it is still possible to find a way to resolve the matter. This case is still worth paying close attention to. The authorities are keeping the details of the negotiations on this case a secret, probably because they are still under investigation and have not yet reached the stage where they can be disclosed. The protest previously lodged by the Japanese Consul in Shantou was refuted by our side with various points of suspicion, and the Japanese side then agreed to have experts investigate the true cause of Kakuda's death, while also asking our side to assist in the search for the murderer. What remains to be investigated in this case is the evidence presented by the Japanese side that Kakuda was sniped, such as: the two blood-stained bullets removed from the corpse by Japanese doctors at the Japanese Philanthropic Hospital; the injury report on the surface of the corpse examined by British doctor Hall at the Gospel Hospital; the photos of the bullet holes on the wall where the deceased fell in Mingde Lane; and the photo of the threatening letter received by Kakuda from the anti-smuggling team before his death. Our side has also raised several points of suspicious evidence, such as: none of the residents near Lianhe Lane and Mingde Lane heard any gunshots at the time; there were no bloodstains at the spot where the deceased fell; the Japanese Philanthropic Hospital refused to allow police officer Shi Guopan to accompany the body upstairs; the removal of the bullets from the corpse was not supervised by our side; why was it necessary to rush to remove the bullets from the corpse; having already been taken to the hospital and died, why wait two hours before reporting the case; the bullet wound in the corpse was slanted downwards, the bullet entered the body and turned before exiting; the wound only had some small congealed blood. All of these are suspicious, and experts urgently need to investigate them. It is heard that the case has now been transferred to Guangzhou for negotiation.

On February 1, the Japanese Navy, due to the Kakuda incident, dispatched two additional warships, "Akikaze" and "Hamakaze," to Shantou, bringing the total number of Japanese warships in Shantou to five, seemingly as a show of surveillance. Lieutenant General Kajikawa traveled from Hong Kong to Guangzhou on the 4th, ostensibly for a courtesy visit, but it is said that he was actually carrying out a major mission, which was to persuade the authorities to expand the organization for autonomy and anti-communism, and to increase the centrifugal force of the Southwest against the Central Government. In short, the Kakuda incident in Shantou at this time is a hidden danger, and the situation may escalate at any time. The three Japanese warships "Yubari," "Hayabusa," and "Ume" that had been in Shantou for a long time suddenly left Shantou for Xiamen on the 2nd, but the Japanese side has not relaxed its grip on the Chaoshan area.

Gansu Provincial Government Stipulates Plan for Conscripting Labor 71

Dedicated to Road Building, River Dredging, and Afforestation, with Strict Orders for All Agencies to Comply

Lanzhou News, Provincial Government Chairman Yu Xuezhong previously received the "Outline of Winter Labor Conscription Measures" promulgated by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. Although civil servants in the provincial capital and people in various counties have already implemented labor service one after another, the overall labor conscription for all agencies, armies, schools, and people in the province has not yet been implemented. Therefore, the Construction Department was instructed to formulate the "Gansu Province 24th Year Winter Labor Conscription Plan," which consists of seven items, and stipulates that the period from November 1, 1935, to the end of March 1936 shall be the labor conscription period. It is heard that it has been reported to the Executive Yuan and sent to the Garrison Commander of Gansu and Suiyuan and the Second Route Army Headquarters for compliance. The plan is recorded as follows:

The winter labor conscription period for this year is set from November 1, 1935, to the end of March 1936.

This year's labor conscription work will be carried out in various projects as follows, to be completed on schedule: (A) Road construction, (1) Ganqing Highway, Lanzhou to Xiangtang section (2) Lintao to Tianshui branch road (3) Longxi to Minxian branch road (B) Canal dredging, (1) Tao Hui Canal in Lintao County (2) Tong Hui Canal in Yongdeng and Gaolan Counties (3) Yongfengchuan Canal in Yongjing County (C) Afforestation, first plant roadside trees along the sides of motor vehicle and railway tracks in each county, plant bank protection forests along river embankments, and plant as much as possible on barren mountains and wastelands.

The estimated amount of various labor conscription projects for this year is as follows: (A) Road construction, in addition to the collection of funds for the construction of stone bridges and culverts and special projects, the amount of earthwork is estimated separately as follows: (1) Ganqing Highway, Lanzhou-Xiangtang section, 123 kilometers long, with a road width of 9 meters (total earthwork of more than 807,000 cubic meters). (2) Lintao to Tianshui branch road, 261 kilometers long, with a road width of 7.5 meters, with a total earthwork of more than 1,295,000 cubic meters. (3) Longxi to Minxian branch road, 115 kilometers long, with a road width of 7.5 meters, with a total earthwork of more than 1,035,000 cubic meters. (B) Canal excavation, in addition to the borrowing of funds for dams, sluices, bridges, culverts, and special projects, the amount of earthwork for each canal is estimated as follows: (1) Tao Hui Canal, 29 kilometers long, with a total earthwork of more than 228,000 cubic meters. (2) Tong Hui Canal, 71 kilometers long, with a total earthwork of 302,000 cubic meters. (3) Yongfengchuan Canal, 29 kilometers long, with a total earthwork of 425,000 cubic meters. (C) Afforestation, (1) first-class counties must plant at least 100,000 trees each, 6 counties totaling 600,000 trees, (2) second-class counties must plant at least 80,000 trees each, 41 counties totaling 3,280,000 trees, (3) third-class counties must plant at least 50,000 trees each, 20 counties totaling 1,000,000 trees.

The estimated number of labor days required for this year's winter labor conscription work is as follows: (A) Road construction, Ganqing Road Lanzhou-Xiangtang section, requires 500,000 labor days; Lintao to Tianshui Highway, requires 900,000 labor days; Longxi to Minxian Highway, requires 700,000 labor days. (B) Canal excavation, Tao Hui Canal, requires 150,000 labor days; Tong Hui Canal, requires 210,000 labor days; Yongfengchuan Canal, requires 280,000 labor days. (C) Afforestation, the entire province must plant 4,880,000 trees, each labor day can plant 2,000 trees, requiring a total of 244,000 labor days.

The distribution of the progress of various labor conscription projects for this year is as follows: (A) Road construction, the Lanzhou-Xiangtang section of the Ganqing Highway will be undertaken by the labor of Gaolan and Yongdeng counties; the Lintao to Tianshui Highway will be divided among the labor of Lintao, Weiyuan, Longxi, Wushan, Gangu, and Tianshui counties; the Longxi to Minxian Highway will be undertaken by the labor of Longxi and Minxian counties. (B) Canal excavation, the Tao Hui Canal will be undertaken by the labor of Lintao County; the Tong Hui Canal will be undertaken by the labor of Gaolan and Yongdeng counties; the Yongfengchuan Canal will be undertaken by the labor of Yongjing County. (C) Afforestation, all 67 counties and bureaus in the province should review the local climate, decide on the conscription of labor, and carry out afforestation universally. Yongjing, Fulan, Yuzhong, Jingyuan, Jingtai, and Yongdeng counties along the river should pay more attention to bank protection afforestation.

The supervision and management methods for various labor conscription projects for this year are stipulated as follows: (A) Road construction and canal excavation, the Construction Department will dispatch engineering technicians to supervise and guide respectively, and the county governments along the road will supervise and instruct the township chiefs to conscript labor according to the household register, organizing 50 people as a group for group management, and construct according to the plan diagrams. After completion, the Construction Department will send personnel to inspect and accept, and report to the provincial government for rewards and punishments according to the merits of the results. (B) Afforestation, the county government should distribute the number of trees to be planted according to the regulations, according to the number of Baos and Jias in each county, and the head of each Lianbao is responsible for supervision. After the completion of the project, the head of each Jia shall report to the Lianbao head in charge for summary, and report to the county government for review and verification, and then report to the Construction Department, which will send personnel to investigate, distinguish the results, and present a list to the provincial government for rewards and punishments.

The completion deadlines for various labor conscription projects for this year are stipulated as follows: (A) Road construction, the Lanzhou-Xiangtang section of the Ganqing Road is scheduled to be fully completed by the end of March 1936; the Lintao to Tianshui Highway is scheduled to be fully completed by the end of March 1936; the Longxi to Minxian Highway is scheduled to be fully completed by the end of March 1936. (B) Canal excavation, the Tao Hui Canal is scheduled to be half completed by the end of March 1936 and fully completed by the end of June; the Tong Hui Canal is scheduled to be one-quarter completed by the end of March 1936 and fully completed by the end of December; the Yongfengchuan Canal is scheduled to be one-quarter completed by the end of March 1936 and fully completed by the end of December. (C) Afforestation, the completion period is delayed due to the late festival in Gansu Province, up to the time around the Grain Rain in 1936.

Guangdong Province Rectifies Salt Affairs 72

Salt Tax Revenue Shrinking Year by Year, Improving Salt Production, Constructing Central Warehouse, Newly Setting Salt Catty Distribution and Transportation Methods

Guangdong Correspondence, Guangdong Province borders the sea, and the South Road and Dongjiang both produce a large amount of salt catties. In the past, in addition to supplying this province, it was also sold to the provinces of Guangxi, Hunan, Fujian, and Jiangxi. However, in recent years, sales have decreased greatly. The reason is that Guangxi Province has the adulteration of Vietnamese sea salt, and the Hunan market is monopolized by Huai salt. Only the borders of Fujian and Jiangxi still have some sales markets, but they are far less than in the past. It is found that the total revenue of Guangdong salt tax in 1933 was more than 13 million, only 10 million in 1934, and only more than 9.2 million last year (1935). Judging from this situation, there is a trend of shrinking year by year. Recently, the Guangdong Salt Affairs Audit Office and the Liangguang Salt Transportation Envoy Office have urgently planned relief methods to improve the production and transportation of salt catties. On the one hand, technical experts are hired to go to various salt fields to guide the improvement of salt drying methods, and on the other hand, in order to facilitate transportation, a salt storage central warehouse is being built near the Yuehan Railway in Huangsha, Guangzhou, with a project cost of 200,000 yuan. In the future, if it is completed, salt boats from various places can directly transport the central warehouse in the province for storage, which can save the past suffering of transshipment and storage. In addition, in order to rectify the transportation and sales of salt catties, the Liangguang Salt Transportation Envoy Office has recently formulated temporary measures for the distribution and transportation of salt catties in various fields, which will be announced and implemented starting this month, and the implementation period is temporarily set at six months. The methods are as follows: The purpose of this method is to maintain the 37% transportation quota, adjust the production and sales methods of various fields, abolish the method of stamping and receiving process certificates from the guild, allow each merchant to freely report and transport according to the quota, in order to facilitate handling and avoid disputes. The stipulation of the 37% transportation quota is temporarily based on the average number of actual sales in the province in the past five years. The salt fields in the east and west account for 70%, and the salt fields in Leiqiong account for 30%. Each merchant is allowed to freely report and transport within the quota, but the annual standard total quota is still divided into four phases, and the total number of distributions and transportations for each merchant in each phase must not exceed the fixed quota for that phase, and the actual distribution number to the field must not exceed 10% of the distribution number filled in the process certificate, in order to prevent the malpractice of excessive transportation and congestion, and the government can still change the handling according to the needs of the sales market at any time. The standard quota is determined in another table. Each merchant can freely receive and transport salt at the beginning of each phase of salt transportation. However, for Leiqiong salt catties, each merchant can freely report the number of distributions and transportations first, and after ten days, the number of reports and transportations from each merchant will be summarized and then issued a water process certificate separately, but it is stipulated that if the total number of reports and transportations from each merchant at the same time exceeds the fixed quota for that phase, the total number can be converted separately according to the number of reports and transportations from each merchant, and each merchant will be informed separately and allowed to freely assemble and transport in rotation and jointly report to receive the water process certificate. Those with a small number that are not easy to assemble and transport are allowed to hire sailboats for towing. After the transportation quota is allocated, if there are those who do not receive the process certificate for distribution and transportation, the government can consider the number of Leiqiong salt in the province and temporarily change the unfulfilled transportation quota to the second one who receives the process certificate for transportation in order to take care of the sales market. For the distribution and transportation of Leiqiong salt catties, the validity period of the process certificate and the date of reporting and transportation have been slightly less strictly regulated in the past, and it is inevitable that there are malpractices such as delaying reporting and distribution after receiving the process certificate. Additional regulations should be added: all transport ships must report to the field for transportation and distribution within 15 days after receiving the process certificate, and return to the province within 8 days; sailboats must complete the distribution within 30 days and return to the province within 20 days. If the problem is not declared and the deadline is exceeded, the process certificate will be cancelled, and the loss will be borne by the merchant himself, and those who have distributed salt will still be investigated and punished according to regulations, in order to take measures. During the distribution period of the 37% fixed quota, the transportation halls in the east and west fields are not restricted from being freely established, but the transportation halls in Leiqiong are restricted from increasing. This is a temporary expedient measure. Now, in order to publicly tow and avoid involving patents, all merchants who want to establish new Leiqiong transportation halls are allowed to freely report and handle the matter according to the regulations without adding restrictions, but in order to stabilize the business of existing Leiqiong transporters, after the new merchant is approved to establish a hall, the newly established hall cannot occupy the right to transport salt in the current 30% transportation quota, and must wait until the next 30% transportation quota begins before participating in receiving the process certificate for salt transportation in order to maintain order and avoid patents. The method of stopping ships in the east and west salt fields is abolished, and it is related to the self-interest of the east field merchants, so the east and west field merchants are allowed to freely gather to discuss and resolve the matter and report for approval. Leiqiong transporters do not need to invest in purchasing process ships to establish transportation halls, and their qualifications for transporting salt are very different from those of east and west field transporters, who must purchase several large process ships as a guarantee before they can establish halls for salt transportation. The burdens are also different. Currently, the construction of Leiqiong salt warehouses in the province's rivers requires a lot of money, which cannot be raised. It is planned to collect 5 cents per package of Leiqiong salt catties reported for transportation as a fee for building Leiqiong salt warehouses. All Leiqiong salt catties distributed for transportation should be handed over to the accounting office of this office for verification and collection at the time of receiving the process certificate according to the number of salt transported, and a receipt will be given. When the salt ship returns to the province, after clearing the warehouse, the actual number of distributions will be verified and the amount will be supplemented accordingly. This method is temporarily drafted and will be implemented on a trial basis for six months. It should be abolished or continued to be handled at the time of expiration. If there are any matters that are not exhausted in this method, and there are any changes that should be made, this office will consider and approve them at any time. (February 3)

Recent Bandit Situation in Eastern and Western Fujian

Fuzhou Correspondence, A large number of bandits have recently been discovered in the Taishun and Qingyuan areas of western Zhejiang, with a total of 500 to 600 people and 500 to 600 guns.
