Smokers Entering the City from Other Provinces and Cities Must Obtain a License from the Public Security Bureau 122

Severe Punishment for Those Found without a License, Regardless of the Duration of Stay

Public Notice from the Municipal Public Security Bureau: It has been found that this city is a national commercial center with many merchants and travelers coming and going. Among them, there are many who are addicted to opium smoking. Since the Bureau began registering smokers, very few registered smokers from other provinces and cities who move to or travel to this city have exchanged their licenses or travel permits with the Bureau. The reason for this is either ignorance of the anti-smoking laws and the procedures for exchanging licenses, or intentional evasion due to the short duration of the trip, hoping to conceal the addiction. These loopholes have a serious impact on the anti-smoking policy. Those who hold ordinary limited-term smoking cessation licenses must, if moving to this city, follow the provisions of Article 8 of the Regulations on the Strict Implementation of Smoking Cessation and the Prohibition of Addicts, bring their original license to the Bureau for cancellation, and apply for a limited-term license for this city. The Bureau will then send the cancelled license to the original county or city for cancellation. If they are traveling temporarily and staying for less than three months, they can exchange their original license for a travel permit from the Bureau. Those who hold poor people's limited-term smoking cessation licenses must follow the provisions of item D of Article 5 of the Measures for the Limited-Term Registration of Addicts, bring their poor people's smoking cessation license from their original county or city to the Bureau to apply for a seal to continue using it. The regulations for exchanging licenses and permits are extremely detailed, and the Bureau, in charge of important anti-smoking policies, cannot be lenient. In the future, all registered smokers from other provinces and cities who move to or travel to this city, regardless of the duration of their stay, must comply with the above procedures and exchange their licenses and permits with the Bureau. Those who evade or conceal their addiction and fail to comply will be severely punished according to the law. In addition to issuing orders to subordinate units to conduct strict inspections at any time, this notice is hereby issued for public knowledge and compliance. This notice.

President Luo of the Court Instructs the Bar Association to Clarify the Issue of Trial Time 123

Mutual Understanding of Factual Difficulties, the Establishment of a Question Office is Highly Usable

The Shanghai Bar Association held an executive supervisory meeting the night before last. Zhang Yongqing, a member of the association, reported to the Shanghai District Court that the court was not punctual in hearing criminal cases and did not notify lawyers to appear in court to defend simple criminal cases, requesting that the association forward a letter to correct these issues. The matter was published in the newspapers. Luo, the president of the Shanghai District Court, read the report and believed that there was some misunderstanding regarding the points raised by the lawyer. Yesterday, he instructed the Shanghai Bar Association, "To the matter of the notification, I have recently read in the newspapers that the association convened the 217th joint meeting, listing several items requesting the court to correct. The court will gladly accept any matter that is beneficial to the convenience of the parties. However, the court handles many civil and criminal cases every day. The points raised by member Zhang Yongqing, as passed by the association, may be occasionally true, but there are factual difficulties. It would be regrettable to generalize from one or two examples. The member did not specify the date, court, or case, so the court cannot investigate. Because the matter is important, I hereby instruct the association to explain each point raised by the member and include the following corrective measures: Regarding the time of civil and criminal court hearings, each presiding judge should arrive in court on time. However, due to the order of cases, if Case A is scheduled for 9 AM and Case B is scheduled for 10 AM, and sometimes Case A is more complicated or the lawyers representing both sides debate for a longer time, and one hour is not enough to complete the inquiry, then the opening time of Case B will inevitably be slightly delayed. As for the execution of cases, each judge of this court summons more than thirty cases every day. At the time of each hearing, the cases are tried in court according to the rules. These are all real situations. In the future, if lawyers have doubts about the opening of the court, they can directly submit them to the president of the court. If they have doubts about the execution of cases, they can directly inquire in writing, and the reasons will be answered. Regarding the delivery of verdicts, there have been some delays during holidays, which have been strictly rectified. In the future, they will be delivered on time. In simple criminal cases, the appointed defenders often submit their letters of appointment the day before or on the day of the hearing, so the court does not have time to notify them in writing, but still notifies them to appear in court in a simple way. There has been no case of failing to notify lawyers. Furthermore, in order to facilitate the progress of cases and streamline procedures, a question office has been established with question books and question forms. Lawyers can list facts and make statements to the question office at any time for verification. It is hereby ordered that the association be notified. This order."

The Department of Health Will Hold a Dentist Examination 124

Registration Before April 5th

Liu Ruiheng, the Director of the Department of Health, considering that the qualifications of practicing dentists in various localities are inconsistent, urgently needs to promulgate regulations for management. He has drafted the Provisional Rules for the Management of Dentists and the Measures for the Examination of Dentists, which were submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval and promulgated and implemented on October 1, 1935. All practicing dentists in various localities who do not meet the qualifications of dentists stipulated in the current rules must first undergo an examination. Those who pass the examination and obtain a certificate can also apply for a dentist's certificate. The first dentist examination has been scheduled for April 20th. Those who are registered with local government agencies to practice dentistry, or who have studied at a registered person's business for more than three years, must submit their credentials, photographs, resumes, and fees to the Department before April 5th for review, in order to participate in the upcoming dentist examination.

Beijing-Shanghai Railway: Telegraph Line Modification Completed 132

All Formally Notified

Xinxin News Agency reports: The Beijing-Shanghai Railway telegraph line has been modified by the Railway Bureau's Mechanical Department, which has added Wuxi Station to the original direct telegraph line, converting it into an express line. The original small sound telegraph line and train report line have been merged, and Anting, Weiting, Wangting, Henglin, and Benniu stations have been converted into relay stations. The small sound telegraph line has been converted into a direct telegraph line, and Danyang and Kunshan stations have been added in addition to the original stations. The entire project was completed on January 20 of this year. The department has also installed a small telegraph machine each at Sanmin Road and Sanmin Road Branch Station, connecting Jiangwan and Gaojingmiao stations, which was also completed and reported on the 22nd of the same month.

Collection Method: One Copper Coin Per Teapot Sold; One Yuan Per Month for Water Sales Starting March 1st

Attendees included Li Shengxian from Shunxingyuan, Liu Peilin from Jinshengyuan, Wang Yucai from Hengleyuan, and dozens of others. Wu, the general captain of the headquarters (represented by Li Dachao), Zhang Yuliang, and Chen Shuo presided over the meeting. Captain Wu (represented by Li) reported, stating briefly, "We have invited everyone here today to discuss the implementation of collecting national aviation salvation funds from the boiled water industry in this city. The general captain was unable to attend due to other matters and is represented by me. Your industry's patriotic enthusiasm in suggesting support for the aviation salvation fundraising campaign and collecting national aviation salvation funds is greatly appreciated. In the first fundraising campaign in March 1933, we received enthusiastic support from all sectors of the city, raising over 1.3 million in just a few months and enrolling 100,000 members to purchase airplanes, assist the government, and strengthen national defense. In March of last year, this city continued to hold the second fundraising drive. Various industries, including your industry, the hotel industry, the butchering industry, the vending industry, and the fresh meat industry, which began collecting national aviation salvation funds during the first fundraising campaign, are still in the process. Recently, the freight trucking industry, the sand and gravel industry, the yellow sand and crushed stone industry, the brick and ash industry, the dance hall industry, the civilian ship industry, the coal and stone barge industry, and the restaurants have successively suggested collecting national aviation salvation funds based on the standard of business revenue, and the progress has been excellent. Your industry should unite, concentrate its efforts to promote aviation salvation, and do its best to raise national aviation salvation funds. If anyone has any opinions, we hope you will express them freely." Subsequently, Li Sheng, Chen Dianshi, and Che Lisheng from the industry's guild spoke one after another, stating briefly, "The collection of national aviation salvation funds is a matter of supporting the aviation salvation movement. We are citizens and should do our best to fulfill our duties." After which, it was discussed and decided that tea sellers would collect one copper coin per teapot, and those selling water alone would collect one yuan in national currency per month, starting on March 1st, which was unanimously approved. A photograph was then taken, and the meeting adjourned at 6:30 PM.

Military Cap Industry Labor-Contracting Dispute 135

Party and Government Agencies Will Mediate According to Law

Dagong News Agency reports: The military cap labor-contracting parties in this city, in July of last year, signed a labor-contracting agreement for the 25th year at the Social Affairs Bureau. The contractor Zhong Changyuan and others contracted to produce 220,000 spring military caps this year. In order to fulfill the contract, the contractor submitted a request to the Social Affairs Bureau, ordering the Shanghai Military Uniform Workers' Union to instruct its military cap industry members to go to work. After receiving the request, the Social Affairs Bureau immediately ordered the union to instruct its members to go to work. The union, upon receiving the order, selected six tailoring workers and forty-eight sewing workers, each carrying a sewing machine, and brought them with instructions to the military cap factory at Kangti Lane, Kangti Fang in the French Concession. Unexpectedly, when the workers arrived at the factory gate, the contractor not only did not allocate work, but also closed the factory gate tightly, not allowing the workers to enter the factory. Seeing that the contractor Zhong Changyuan and others were openly violating government orders, the workers elected representatives to petition party and government agencies, and the Municipal Party Department sent Fan Guoren and the Social Affairs Bureau sent Zhao Lian to mediate, but without result. Furthermore, a large number of detectives were sent by the French Concession police to disperse the workers and detain all the sewing machines. Representatives of party and government agencies believe that the contractor Zhong Changyuan and others first requested the government to order the union to send workers to work, and then defied the order and refused to employ them, which is greatly dissatisfied. It is planned to schedule a mediation. The military uniform union, considering the contractor's inconsistent behavior, reliance on the concession, and violation of the contract, causing great losses to the workers, has decided to collect evidence, hire Zhou Lianze as a lawyer, and legally pursue various losses.

Sichuan Opera to be Broadcast in Shanghai 138

This city's business is prosperous, and it is close to the capital, making it a gathering place for people from all provinces. All kinds of theatrical entertainment, such as Cantonese opera, Beijing opera, and even northern miscellaneous tunes, are available. However, Sichuan opera has never been performed here due to the long distance. Sichuan opera originated before the Song Dynasty and was popularized and promoted by the famous Sichuan scholar Su Dongpo, making it popular in Sichuan. Its elegant lyrics and melodious tunes have a unique flavor and are highly praised by people from all provinces who have been to Sichuan. Recently, several members of the most famous Sanqinghui Opera Troupe in Sichuan have been hired by the Shanghai Victory Record Company to come to Shanghai to record records. Sichuan stores in this city, taking advantage of the troupe's presence in Shanghai, have requested the troupe as a friendly gesture to broadcast on the radio in Shanghai for a few days in the near future to satisfy the ears of the people in Shanghai. The date of broadcast will be announced later. Sichuan stores have also printed and distributed Sichuan opera lyrics for the convenience of those with radios to listen. Anyone who wishes to read them can obtain them from the Sichuan Store headquarters at the intersection of Daimalu and Shanxi Road or the Sichuan Store branch at the Throwing Ball Field.

Minor Delinquencies Must Also be Cleared Monthly

Shenshi News Agency reports: The Shanghai Bamboo Industry Guild issued a notice stating that due to the sluggish market, declining business, tight credit, and difficult turnover in recent years, it is impossible to survive without seeking improvement. Letters to the Editor 149

Dear Editor, After reading the Da Mei Evening News of January 19th regarding the news of the Ministry of Industry's relief for sericulture, it stated, "Last year, the price of silk abroad soared, so silk factories had considerable surpluses. Factory shutdowns were frequent, but some silk factories intentionally shut down because they currently have more than eight million dan of silk in storage, which can be maintained until the new silkworms come on the market." This news is absolutely untrue. Whether silk factories had considerable surpluses or intentionally shut down is not true. At that time, the investigation of silk stored in Shanghai was only over two thousand dan, which is not comparable to the so-called eight million dan. Also, the Xinwen Daily News reported on January 27th that eight silk factories opened that day, and on January 28th, the newspaper reported that nine silk factories opened. According to the facts, they are not in accordance with reality. At that time, not a single silk factory in Shanghai opened. Last year, although the market was slightly better for silk factories in Shanghai, they did not necessarily have considerable surpluses, and they were mostly forced to shut down due to the impact of restrictions on silk sales in Zhejiang Province and the exhaustion of raw materials. This special letter is sent to you, hoping that you will publish it in the "Letters to the Editor" column to clarify the truth. Sincerely, Shanghai Silk Factory Industry Guild Committee, February 7th.

Dear Editor, My residence in Shanghai was robbed yesterday morning, with losses of only a hundred yuan in cash, over two hundred small coins, two watches, four rings, and a personally owned pistol, totaling no more than three to five hundred yuan, which is far from what was reported. It is because I am an ordinary businessman, serving as the factory director of Yifeng General Factory, not the manager, and my simple residence is far from extravagant. Although I was robbed, it was only a small amount. I respectfully request that my letter be published to clarify the truth. With public friendship, sincerely, Wu Huangxiang, February 8th.

Dear Editor, According to Zhou Weisheng's statement, he was shocked to read the news item "Farmers Accuse Baoshang" in the news column of the Shen Bao on the 7th of this month. The case of my client being falsely accused of enticing lewdness by Zhou Miaogen to the Shanghai District Court has been answered by me according to law, and a counter-accusation of false accusation has been filed. Once the investigation is concluded, the truth will be clear. The sections published in the newspaper are completely inconsistent with the facts. For this reason, I have entrusted your lawyer to write to the newspaper, requesting a correction. Accordingly, I am sending you this letter, hoping that you will investigate and correct it. Sincerely, Attorney Li Zonghong, February.

Weather Report 150

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast for 4:30 PM yesterday: The weather around Shandong is slightly cold, with variable winds, due to an area of high pressure moving eastward from Mongolia. The Yangtze River basin and its vicinity are cloudy and cold, sometimes turning to clouds, with light and directionless winds. There is light fog in the morning. The East China Sea and Taiwan are cloudy, with local rain and winter monsoon. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 36.7 and the lowest was 31.1. On the same day last year, the highest was 46.8 and the lowest was 32.9.

Sino-Belgian Boxer Indemnity Committee to Continue University Thesis Awards 172

Distributes Letters to Domestic University Students to Participate, Allocates 3,000 Yuan as Thesis Awards

The Sino-Belgian Boxer Indemnity Committee has decided to continue the University Thesis Awards this year. It has recently distributed letters to public and private universities in China, soliciting students to actively participate. The details are as follows:

Letters to Universities: The committee recently distributed letters to universities in China, stating that the committee allocates 3,000 yuan annually to encourage academic research as thesis awards for Chinese universities. The topics of the theses and the review matters are handled by experts in the committee. The results of the implementation in the 22nd year were quite successful. This year, the remaining funds will continue to be used. Experts have been hired to propose topics. In addition to publishing them in newspapers, we have enclosed the thesis award rules and a copy of the thesis topics for each department for your review. We hope you will announce this widely to promote friendship.

Award Regulations: The committee allocates 3,000 yuan annually to encourage academic research as thesis awards for Chinese universities. The awards are divided into several types, each with several levels. The committee will issue essay questions, and those with insightful and valuable essays will be awarded a reward based on the evaluation results. In addition to the award money, they will receive a honorary certificate. Those who wish to submit these theses must be graduating students of universities or independent colleges that have been registered in China. Their theses must be related to their major subjects. The types and departments of the theses, and the distribution of the awards, will be decided by the committee's Chinese delegation before soliciting theses each year. The topics and evaluation of the theses will be handled by experts in the committee. The theses must be written in Chinese, but they can also be written in English, German, or French, but must be accompanied by a Chinese translation. If the expert committee believes that none of the theses in each department is worthy of a certain type or level of award, the committee's Chinese delegation may retain that type or level of award as an accumulation of the award. The accumulated funds may be used by the committee, but only for the purpose of encouraging academic research. Detailed rules for the implementation of these regulations will be determined separately. These regulations may be revised by the committee's Chinese delegation.

Exam Questions for Each Department: A. Engineering Department, Mechanical Engineering Department Exam Questions: Mechanical Power Transmission Methods for Vehicles and Factories; What kind of prime mover should be used for a factory with national defense characteristics, and how should it be designed? B. Agricultural Science Department, Agronomy Department: The current situation of cotton in China and the methods of its improvement; Cotton industry and national defense. C. Science Department, Physics Department Exam Questions: Catalog and abstracts of physics papers published by Chinese physicists at home and abroad; Detailed description of various studies of atomic nuclear structure; Raman effect and molecular structure. D. Law Department, Law Department Exam Questions: The difference and relationship between law and morality; Explain its jurisprudence on the establishment and revocation of a contract; What is the reason why British and American scholars do not recognize that an offer has binding force, while the mainland scholars cherish it? E. Business Department, Accounting Department Exam Questions: Overview of cost accounting for textile mills. F. Medical Department, Hygiene Department Exam Questions: The relationship between public health and people's livelihood; How should our country's overall medical and health construction be planned and implemented?

Youth Education Society Declaration (2) 173

In the process of the Northern Expedition, the mass revolution movement led by youth established the foundation for the completion of the Northern Expedition. This was because the youth at that time had a unified and correct goal, knowing that they were seeking the eradication of warlords and the establishment of a unified revolutionary government. Now, times have changed, and the situation is completely different. Youth should first seek a correct understanding and then have correct actions. In summary, the mutual slaughter of imperialists and the anti-aggression wars of oppressed nations will inevitably be unavoidable. Our only preparation is the awakening of the whole people and the soundness of the youth themselves, so that they can win in the future anti-aggression war. The central government has established the road ahead for revolutionary construction. This is a great process for completing the Chinese revolution and a necessary preparation for our anti-aggression war. The power of the revolution is established through the construction of a road. They can gain liberation from future wars. Youth is the foundation of the Chinese revolution. The Chinese revolution is the foundation of China's liberation. China's liberation is the foundation for the liberation of oppressed nations along the Pacific coast. The liberation of oppressed nations along the Pacific coast is the foundation for the liberation of oppressed humanity around the world. Chinese youth, how great is the responsibility here? The soundness of Chinese youth is the foundation of the above-mentioned foundations. The soundness of Chinese youth lies in educational development. Obviously, past Chinese education cannot bear this mission. In extraordinary times, there is education for extraordinary times. In the past, the youth's recognition was not clear about the goals of the Chinese revolution, and they could not determine united revolutionary action. On the contrary, they were easily agitated by passion and incited by villains, dispersing the front of the national revolution. This is the failure of Chinese education. The Chinese youth education in the extraordinary period must make the youth know about the inevitable mutual slaughter of imperialists and the anti-aggression war of oppressed people in the international community, know that revolutionary construction is the foundation for China to win the future anti-aggression war in the country, and know that their own soundness is the condition for completing China's revolutionary construction in themselves. We must review the present, grasp the real problems, implement construction, create the power of struggle, sharpen the ten Qi to develop the great festival of dying for the country, and then can lead the whole people to advance on the revolutionary road under the correct goals.

This is certainly the responsibility of Chinese educators, but it is also the effort that we youth ourselves should have. We must start from our own efforts, start from united organizations, establish Chinese youth education in extraordinary times, and cultivate Chinese youth in extraordinary times. Youths of the Chinese era, the twentieth century is the era of China's liberation. China's liberation is based on the completion of the construction of Chinese youth education. The giant wheel of the times will force us to move forward. The liberation of all oppressed humanity is our responsibility. Youths of the Chinese era, take on this glorious responsibility. Liangjiang Girl Scout Training Class This Season's Expansion Plan 174

Since our country's scouting cause has been vigorously promoted by the government, its achievements have been advancing by leaps and bounds. In the past, schools above the junior high school level across the country were ordered to add scouting courses uniformly. Because there are many schools in the country, the demand for instructors and teachers is high. Liangjiang Girls' Physical Education School in Jiangwan, Shanghai, first created a girl scout instructor training class to engage in cultivation. It has been several years. Since girl scout education is most practical today, we must strive to promote it. Therefore, we have formulated an expansion plan for this season, adding specialized personnel, increasing equipment courses, and focusing on labor and housework to instill the various knowledge and skills that women need most. Since the enrollment began, many letters from various places have inquired about the information and registered.

Little Boy (1) (7) (1) 176

— Among the children, except for Fulan and Shoumi, no one knew what had happened. When they ran downstairs the next morning, they were truly shocked and felt extremely uneasy. The mansion seemed lonely and deserted without its master and mistress. Breakfast was no longer the happy occasion with Mrs. Shu officiating at the tea ceremony. Instead, it was a dull and tasteless meal. When class time arrived, Mr. Pei's seat was also empty. They wandered around for about an hour, feeling lost and unable to console themselves, waiting for news and hoping that Little Qiao's father was not in danger, because the good man John Bullock was deeply loved by the children. Ten o'clock had already arrived, but no one came to alleviate their doubts. They didn't want to play, but time seemed to pass too slowly. They were restless, feeling bored and worried. Suddenly, Fulan stood up and said in his usual moving words: "Hey, I have an idea, children! Let's go to the classroom and do our homework as if Uncle is still here. That way, time will pass faster, and I know it will also make him happy." "But who will listen to us read?" Jake asked. "I will, although what I know is not much more than what you know, but I am the oldest here. If you don't mind, I will try to be his substitute until he comes back."

Therefore, the trend for serge is quite tight. The prices of flannel sets and suits have risen the most, because the piece goods industry is mostly involved in real business, does not prepare extra fabric, and only trades in samples with cash. They will not sell unless they recover their full cost. Even the old goods in stock must be priced up to equal the new goods. Because the colors are different, and once the tailor's sample is determined, it must be cut. Most of the regular medium-grade materials are mainly Japanese goods, and selling prices have also increased and are selling well, due to the Japanese exchange rate and customs duties. Sales are better for medium-grade than for flannel suits. This is because piece goods stores do not have a sufficient inventory and urgently need to sell, unlike suit shops, which still have goods in stock for comparison. Miscellaneous News: Beihai Fennel Continues to Rise, Already Up Six Yuan From Before. There is still a rising trend. The price of Beihai fennel was weak last winter, reaching 24 to 25 yuan. Recently, the market has shifted and prices have risen step by step. The opening price at the first market was 28.8 yuan. The drugstore industry bought in at the highest price. It then rose to 30 yuan. Yesterday, it was heard that the market price had reopened at 31 yuan, a total increase of 6 yuan. However, the goods available are already scarce, and it is heard that production prices in Shanghai need to be 35 to 36 yuan. Therefore, the asking price has increased again. The market is sure to continue to rise. Silk and Tea: Hopes for Chinese Tea Trade with Russia Dashed. The Chinese tea trade with Russia, which was prosperous in the past, had total annual sales reaching over one million boxes. Even ten years ago, the number of red and green tea imported into Russia was 300,000 to 400,000 boxes. Since the Soviet Union implemented its Five-Year Plans twice, it has only purchased tea that is cheap, causing Chinese tea to be replaced by Japan, India, and Java in the Russian market. More recently, the Soviet Union has been actively promoting domestic tea production, establishing over 50 tea plantations. Once self-sufficiency is achieved, foreign tea imports will be eliminated. Last year, Russian firms in Shanghai and Hankou only purchased over 20,000 boxes of red tea from Qimen and Ningzhou in the Hunan and Hubei provinces. Not a single leaf of green tea was imported. It is heard that the Soviet Union plans to further restrict tea imports this year, with a limit of only 500,000 gold rubles, a reduction of six-tenths compared to the past. The current price is 200 yuan, an increase of 10 yuan from before. It is heard that yarn factories are deeply concerned about running out of stock. Yesterday, another four boxes were purchased. 90-Pound English Tinplate Out of Stock. Recently, 90-pound English tinplate has suddenly run out of stock in the market. Shanghai Longwen Bookstore Issues Modern Elementary School Application Forms and Books 177

The Longwen Bookstore of Shanghai's Dananmen recently issued modern elementary school application forms and books, totaling several thousand kinds. They are very new and suitable for use, with printed instructions and price lists included. Requests will be mailed promptly. A complete set of sample books requires one silver dollar. In recent days, many elementary schools in various places have purchased and prepared them.

Guohua Middle School Gathers Excellent Teachers 178

Guohua Middle School on Gordon Road, Shanghai, this semester has been taken over by the alumni association of National Southeastern University, National Jiaotong University, and National Central University. Tian Ding'an has been invited to serve as the principal, and efforts have been made to improve and expand school affairs. In addition to establishing scholarships, experienced experts from various universities at home and abroad have been re-employed to serve as faculty and staff. This includes Zhang Zitau, a graduate of the Education Department of the former National Nanjing Higher Normal School, who previously served as a teacher at Jiangsu Provincial Vocational Normal School, the Provincial Second and Third Normal Schools, and Yangzhou Middle School, as well as the director of the Taixian Education Bureau in Jiangsu, and a staff member of the Shanghai Education Bureau, who will serve as the director of teaching affairs; Wang Ruli, a Master of Science from MIT, will serve as a physics and chemistry teacher; Run Shouzhong, a Bachelor of Arts from Tsinghua University, and Lin Yunqiu, a Bachelor of Arts from Ginling Women's University, will serve as English teachers; Sun Jiarui, a Bachelor of Commerce from Central University, will serve as the head of the business department; Zhuang Guoxi, a Bachelor of Agriculture from Central University, will serve as a biology and labor teacher; Liu Baozong, a Bachelor of Arts from Central University, will serve as a history and geography teacher; Zhu Zhichao, a graduate of Peiyang University, will serve as a mathematics teacher. As for the director of affairs, Lu Zhuocheng, a graduate of Jiangsu Provincial College of Education; Zhao Hanbo, the director of physical education; Zhu Zubao, with a Bachelor of Arts from Zhejiang University; and Li Chengyun and Xu Xiaodong, with Bachelor of Arts degrees from Fudan University, all have rich knowledge and experience and are invaluable talents. It is said that in addition to hiring experts to serve as faculty and staff, the school has also established lectureships in various disciplines, specially inviting leaders from domestic academic organizations and specialized scholars to serve as lecturers. Furthermore, within less than half a month of the school's takeover, applications from near and far have been very enthusiastic, which is sufficient to prove that people in society deeply believe that the school's future development is limitless.
